<Text>It is very difficult for a cookie to impress me but this one did. I have not had cookies that have a similar taste profile where you can truly taste the browned butter and sea salt. It also has the right amount of crumbly and density, like shortbread but more airy. Highly recommend the original. The gluten free choc mint did not disappoint as well. It wasn't overly sweet and neither the chocolate nor the mint was overpowering, instead they complemented the base recipe well. Only wished we had gotten more. < review>
Small family owned shop with hearty, healthy mostly fruit based snacks. It is Spanish themed but all cultures will find something delicious. Just ask the staff and they'll help you pick something and customize it for you. Our family has tried yummy cheese sauce loaded nachos, smoothie and agua frescas (made to order), Bionicos (chopped fruit, cream and granolla) corn on the cob, veggie wrap (lots of lettuce and hummus) coconut shave ice and their home made fruit popsicles. Everything was fresh and really tasty. The young man and lady working there had great customer service. We highly reccomend it especially on a hot day.</review>

<Review>Golden Koi did a great job of accommodating protocols during Covid. Everyone had to wear gloves when serving themselves.  I normally do not like going to buffets because the thought of people eating and kicking their fingers and going back for seconds and touching the serving spoon with locked fingers is a disgusting thought.  But because everyone had to use gloves to serve themselves,  this thought was diminished. The food was good and being a seafood eater, there were plenty of selections to choose from. <Review>UPDATE!  The Koi Buffet is now open again! It's all the same great food as before. I just can't see the negative reviews here, cause service is great and the place is clean. The food is all fresh if you get here at a reasonable time. Best time is when they open! Fresh food and nobody has picked over all the food yet!  I gotta go back for those wings and ribs!

Closed for now due to the virus thing, but I really can't wait till it opens again! This is the best buffet in the area for a reasonable price. It's under new management so it cleaner than before and the service is perfect. The food is a generous selection of Chinese foods that you don't normally see at most buffets.

What I really like are the fried chicken wings and the ribs! Yeah Chinese do the best Chicken and Ribs! They even have french fries here, just in case you don't want Chinese food. I've always found the food hot and fresh, but do go 1/2 hr before closing and expect all fresh food just for you, it won't happen. Go at opening 11am! <Review>Pretty happy decision to eat there. Looked at the food before deciding and about 8/10 things looked pretty fresh. This was on a Thursday evening so maybe not the most busy time. At least not very busy when we were there. I imagine weekends to be busier.

This place is pretty big. Could seat many people if needed. Food was good and I think it's cool they have soft serve and regular ice cream.

Mostly pretty typical Asian buffet stuff with a few surprises. The Mei Fun was nice! Thin little rice noodles with a simple and warm flavor.

I might come back if I'm in the area and looking for a buffet again. Sushi wasn't great here but most non sushi buffets that offer it generally meet a low expectation for that.

Solid 4 stars. Service was friendly too! Maybe even more so than most buffets. I'll give them credit there.

5 stars if the sushi were better and more of the food items were fresh. But the price is quite good for what you're getting.

Maybe it's tough for buffets to compete at this price range though because Thunder Valley does a buffet that is bigger and about the same price for dinner on weekdays. Between the two, I'd have to give it to thunder but for the sake of variety I'd probably come here from time to time if I frequented this area a lot more.< /Review>< Pics>

<user>109729702180315960873</user>< Name>
Tran T< /Name>
<date>1491686364606< /date><Rate>4< /Rate>< Review>
I am not sure why the others are saying the food isn't fresh and delicious.  It is every visit for me.  It must be the day and time of day I usually go (Sunday, about 1pm).  Everything is fresh and hot.  They couldn't restock crabs ü¶Ä fast enough. I enjoyed just about everything I normally would order at Chinese restaurants. I don't get food poisoning from eating there.

Three things I don't care for there: salad bar, sushi, and the grill to order meat. 1) Chinese food isn't about salad, it's about cook veggies. Don't eat that raw greens at buffet. 2) sushi is Japanese food. Chinese are notoriously bad at making sushi. If you ever had bad sushi, chances are the owner of that place is Chinese or Vietnamese.  3) I watch those guys grill...not sure what it is but they manage to burn the meat all the time. Plus they don't change tongs between raw and cooked meat. That's just asking for trouble. Avoid these 3 and you'll have a more enjoyable experience.

I dock a star for crappy service, as it is expected of Asian restaurants to have crappy service.<//Review>

<Review>The service was wonderful, the people were very friendly, and were definitely on top of things. As for the food, it's mostly seafood oriented, so if you can't eat seafood or don't generally enjoy it, the number of items is severely limited. If you are a seafood buff, it looks very appetizing and I was very excited to see whole cooked crawfish among their selections, not something you generally see west of the Mississippi. I was also happy to see the bean-paste filled items, something my family greatly enjoys when we go to any oriental themed restaurant.
The soft serve ice cream, though, was definitely refreshing, having a vanilla custard flavor that was very delicious as opposed to the run-of-the-mill watered down vanilla you can find standard in a lot of other oriental buffets.
I would've been a lot happier, though, if there had been more beef-based products, or dishes that didn't have fattier-ended meats. The General Tso's chicken is also VERY Americanized, very sweet with very little spicy and sour. My current take-out place wins over The Golden Koi.<//Review><pics>None< /pics>< Resp>
